      * Entry parameters
     C           *ENTRY    PLIST
     C                     PARM           P0RTN   7
     C           P1HMNB    PARM           WP0001  30       BOH Company Num
     C           P1BNNB    PARM           WP0002  70       BOH Buy Order N
     C           P1BONB    PARM           WP0003  50       BOL Load Number
     C           P1CVNB    PARM           WP0004  50       TH Tattoo Numbe
     C           P1B0DT    PARM           WP0005  70       TH Kill Date
     C           P2GENB    PARM           WP0006  50       Tattoo Number N
     C           P3MLST    PARM           WP0007  1        Print Scale Tkt
     C           P4BONW    PARM           WP0008  70       Buy Order New U
     C           P5J7NB    PARM           WP0009  50       Buy Order Load
     C           P6CGDT    PARM           WP0010  70       Kill Date Usr
     C           P7P4ST    PARM           WP0011  1        Status 1
     C           P8OWCD    PARM           WP0012 10        Site Id New
     C           P8DLSS    PARM           WP0013  1        Transfer Site I
     C           P8O3CD    PARM           WP0014  6        Prod Subsidiary
     C           P8DMSS    PARM           WP0015  1        Transfer Subsid
     C           P8V3TX    PARM           WP0016  3        Th State code N
     C           P8DNSS    PARM           WP0017  1        Transfer State
     C           P9DUSS    PARM P9DUSS    WP0018  1        Process EditTat
      *****************************************************************
      * Initialize
     C                     EXSR ZZINIT
      *
      * Exc TrnsfrTtt-AllFiles XF
      * Modification History
     C                     EXSR UASUBR                     Modification Hi
      * Check if this Transfer is for a Repayment
      * Chk Repay in Progress XF - Tattoo Repayment Detail  * 
     C                     CALL 'PWNVXFR'              90  Chk Repay in Pr
     C                     PARM *BLANK    W0RTN   7
     C                     PARM P1HMNB    WQ0001  30       BOH Company Num
     C                     PARM P1BNNB    WQ0002  70       BOH Buy Order N
     C                     PARM P1BONB    WQ0003  50       BOL Load Number
     C                     PARM P1CVNB    WQ0004  50       TH Tattoo Numbe
     C                     PARM P1B0DT    WQ0005  70       TH Kill Date
     C           YL0001    PARM *BLANK    WQ0006  1        TRD Repayment S
     C           YL0002    PARM *BLANK    WQ0007  1        Repayment in Pr
      *
     C           *IN90     IFEQ '1'
      * Call to program ended in error
     C                     MOVEL'Y2U0032' W0RTN
     C                     MOVEL*BLANKS   W0CLPG 10
     C                     MOVEL'PWNVXFR' W0CLPG
      * Send message '*Error occured on CALL...'
     C                     MOVEL'Y2U0032' ZAMSID
     C                     MOVEL'Y2USRMSG'ZAMSGF
     C                     MOVELW0CLPG    ZAMSDA           Message data
     C                     EXSR ZASNMS
     C                     END
      * Error detected?
     C           W0RTN     IFNE *BLANK
     C                     SETON                     99    *
     C                     END

      * HPE056 Payment Type
      * 1/10/96  HPE056   Allow payment type to be update based on
      *                   what the payment status is at the time this
      *                   tattoo is being updated
      * Function Description:  If there are any fields that need to be
      * Changed/Created during the Change functions or Create function
      * Presently: Payment Type

      * that update the Payment Type
      * CASE: PAR.TH Payment Sts is Live anything
     C           TACWST    IFEQ 'ML'                       *IF

     C           TACWST    OREQ 'NL'

     C                     ELSE
      * Release record lock
     C                     UNLCKPKA1CPL1               91  *
     C                     ENDIF

      * Change error detected
     C                     MOVEL'Y2U0004' W0RTN   7
     C                     ELSE
      *
      * DBF change successful
     C                     ENDIF

     C           WMABDT    PARM *ZERO     WQ0023  70       *DATE
     C           WMABTM    PARM *ZERO     WQ0024  60       *TIME
      *
     C           *IN90     IFEQ '1'
      * Call to program ended in error
     C                     MOVEL'Y2U0032' W0RTN
     C                     MOVEL*BLANKS   W0CLPG 10
     C                     MOVEL'PKWDUPC' W0CLPG
      * Send message '*Error occured on CALL...'
     C                     MOVEL'Y2U0032' ZAMSID
     C                     MOVEL'Y2USRMSG'ZAMSGF
     C                     MOVELW0CLPG    ZAMSDA           Message data
     C                     EXSR ZASNMS
     C                     SETON                     99    *
     C                     END
     C                     MOVEL##PGM     WMAGVN           RS Program
     C                     MOVEL##JOB     WMAHVN           RS Job
     C           KLCRSS    KLIST
     C                     KFLD           WMHUNB           LTN Company Num
     C                     KFLD           WMA7DT           LTN Kill Date
     C                     KFLD           WMFHNB           LTN Record Numb
      * Check for duplicate primary key
     C           KLCRSS    SETLL@BSCPFS                  90*
     C           *IN90     IFEQ '1'
     C                     MOVEL'PRK0116' W0RTN   7
      * Send message 'Loss Trans             EX'
     C                     MOVEL'PRK0116' ZAMSID
     C                     EXSR ZASNMS
     C                     GOTO SSEXIT
     C                     ENDIF
      *
     C                     WRITE@BSCPFS                91  *
      *
     C           *IN91     IFEQ '1'
      * Write error detected
     C                     MOVEL'Y2U0004' W0RTN   7
     C                     ELSE
     C                     ENDIF
      *================================================================
     CSR         SSEXIT    ENDSR
      /EJECT
     CSR         STRVGN    BEGSR
      *================================================================

     C                     MOVEL##USR     TSAAVN           RS User Changed

     C                     ENDIF

     C                     UPDAT@DOREU2                91  *
     C                     ELSE
      * Release record lock
     C                     UNLCKPKDOREL0               91  *

      * Change error detected

      * DBF change successful
